```html
<script>
function aiToolsDashboard() {
  return {
    // ìƒíƒœ ë°ì´í„°
    usageStats: { monthlyUsage: 0, remainingCredits: 0, averageQuality: 0, usagePercentage: 0 },
    availableTools: [],
    generationHistory: [],
    filteredGenerations: [],
    
    // UI ìƒíƒœ
    isLoading: false,
    isLoadingHistory: false,
    isProcessing: {},
    showFilters: false,
    filters: { type: '', status: '', period: 'month' },
    
    get canGenerateContent() {
      return this.usageStats.remainingCredits > 0 && !this.isLoading;
    },
    
    // ì´ˆê¸°í™”
    async initDashboard() {
      await Promise.all([
        this.loadUsageStats(),
        this.loadAvailableTools(),
        this.loadGenerationHistory()
      ]);
    },
    
    async loadUsageStats() {
      const response = await fetch('/api/ai-tools/usage-stats');
      if (response.ok) this.usageStats = await response.json();
    },
    
    async loadAvailableTools() {
      const response = await fetch('/api/ai-tools/available');
      if (response.ok) this.availableTools = await response.json();
    },
    
    async loadGenerationHistory() {
      this.isLoadingHistory = true;
      const response = await fetch('/api/ai-tools/generation-history');
      if (response.ok) {
        const result = await response.json();
        this.generationHistory = result.data || [];
        this.applyFilters();
      }
      this.isLoadingHistory = false;
    },
    
    applyFilters() {
      let filtered = [...this.generationHistory];
      if (this.filters.type) filtered = filtered.filter(item => item.type === this.filters.type);
      if (this.filters.status) filtered = filtered.filter(item => item.review_status === this.filters.status);
      this.filteredGenerations = filtered;
    },
    
    // ë„êµ¬ ì‚¬ìš©
    async useTool(toolId) {
      const tool = this.availableTools.find(t => t.id === toolId);
      if (!tool?.enabled) return;
      
      this.$set(this.isProcessing, toolId, true);
      
      const routes = {
        'education_plan': '/ai-tools/education-plan-generation.html',
        'content_generation': '/ai-tools/content-generation.html'
      };
      
      window.location.href = routes[tool.key] || `/ai-tools/${tool.key}.html`;
    },
    
    startQuickGeneration() { window.location.href = '/ai-tools/quick-generation.html'; },
    openSettings() { window.location.href = '/ai-tools/settings.html'; },
    toggleFilter() { this.showFilters = !this.showFilters; },
    refreshHistory() { this.loadGenerationHistory(); },
    
    // ìœ í‹¸ë¦¬í‹°
    getTypeBadgeClass(type) {
      return { 'education_plan': 'badge-blue', 'content': 'badge-green', 'assessment': 'badge-yellow' }[type] || 'badge-gray';
    },
    getTypeText(type) {
      return { 'education_plan': 'êµìœ¡ê³„íš', 'content': 'í•™ìŠµì½˜í…ì¸ ', 'assessment': 'í‰ê°€ìë£Œ' }[type] || type;
    },
    getStatusBadgeClass(status) {
      return { 'completed': 'status-success', 'pending': 'status-warning', 'approved': 'status-success' }[status] || 'status-gray';
    },
    getStatusText(status) {
      return { 'completed': 'ì™„ë£Œ', 'pending': 'ê²€í† ì¤‘', 'approved': 'ìŠ¹ì¸ë¨', 'rejected': 'ë°˜ë ¤ë¨' }[status] || status;
    },
    formatDate(dateString) { return new Date(dateString).toLocaleDateString('ko-KR'); },
    canEdit(item) { return item.review_status !== 'approved'; },
    canDelete(item) { return ['draft', 'rejected'].includes(item.review_status); }
  };
}
</script>
```

#### ì£¼ìš” íŠ¹ì§•
- **ì‹¤ì‹œê°„ í†µê³„**: ì‚¬ìš©ëŸ‰, í¬ë ˆë”§, í’ˆì§ˆ ì§€í‘œ ì‹¤ì‹œê°„ í‘œì‹œ
- **ë„êµ¬ ê·¸ë¦¬ë“œ**: ì‚¬ìš© ê°€ëŠ¥í•œ AI ë„êµ¬ë“¤ ì¹´ë“œ í˜•íƒœë¡œ í‘œì‹œ
- **ìƒì„± ì´ë ¥**: í•„í„°ë§, ì •ë ¬, ê²€ìƒ‰ ê¸°ëŠ¥ ì§€ì›
- **HTMX í†µí•©**: ì‹¤ì‹œê°„ ìƒíƒœ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸
- **Supabase Edge Functions**: AI ë„êµ¬ ë°±ì—”ë“œ í˜¸ì¶œ
- **UTF-8 ì•ˆì „ì„±**: í•œê¸€ ë°ì´í„° ì•ˆì „ ì²˜ë¦¬
- **ì ‘ê·¼ì„±**: ARIA ë ˆì´ë¸”, í‚¤ë³´ë“œ ë„¤ë¹„ê²Œì´ì…˜

```html
    <script>
        // UTF-8 ì•ˆì „ì„± í™•ë³´ í•¨ìˆ˜
        function validateUTF8Text(text) {
            try {
                const encoded = new TextEncoder().encode(text);
                const decoded = new TextDecoder('utf-8', { fatal: true }).decode(encoded);
                return decoded === text;
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('UTF-8 ì¸ì½”ë”© ì˜¤ë¥˜:', error);
                return false;
            }
        }

        // í•œê¸€ í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì•ˆì „ ì²˜ë¦¬
        function safeKoreanText(text) {
            if (!validateUTF8Text(text)) {
                console.warn('UTF-8 ì¸ì½”ë”© ë¬¸ì œê°€ ë°œê²¬ë˜ì—ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤:', text);
                return text.replace(/[\u0000-\u001F\u007F-\u009F]/g, '');
            }
            return text;
        }

        // êµìœ¡ ì½˜í…ì¸  ìƒì„± ìƒíƒœ ê´€ë¦¬ (ìœ„ì— ì •ì˜ëœ êµ¬ì¡° ì‚¬ìš©)
        document.addEventListener('alpine:init', () => {
            Alpine.data('contentGenerationData', () => ({
                ...contentGenerationData,
                
                // í•™ìƒ ê²€ìƒ‰
                searchStudents(query) {
                    if (!query || query.length < 2) return;
                    
                    // HTMXë¥¼ í†µí•œ ì‹¤ì‹œê°„ ê²€ìƒ‰ì€ HTMLì—ì„œ ì²˜ë¦¬
                    console.log('í•™ìƒ ê²€ìƒ‰:', safeKoreanText(query));
                },
                
                // í•™ìƒ ì„ íƒ
                selectStudent(student) {
                    this.selectedStudent = student.id;
                    this.studentContext = {
                        ...student,
                        name: safeKoreanText(student.name)
                    };
                },
                
                // í…œí”Œë¦¿ ë¡œë“œ
                loadTemplates() {
                    return fetch('/api/ai-tools/templates', {
                        method: 'GET',
                        headers: {
                            'Content-Type': 'application/json; charset=utf-8'
                        }
                    })
                    .then(response => response.json())
                    .then(data => {
                        this.templates.categories = data.categories || [];
                    })
                    .catch(error => {
                        console.error('í…œí”Œë¦¿ ë¡œë“œ ì˜¤ë¥˜:', error);
                        this.showError('í…œí”Œë¦¿ì„ ë¶ˆëŸ¬ì˜¤ëŠ” ì¤‘ ì˜¤ë¥˜ê°€ ë°œìƒí–ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.');
                    });
                },
                
                // ì½˜í…ì¸  ìƒì„±
                async generateContent() {
                    this.generationResult.isGenerating = true;
                    this.generationResult.progress = 0;
                    
                    try {
                        const response = await fetch('/api/ai-tools/generate-content', {
                            method: 'POST',
                            headers: {
                                'Content-Type': 'application/json; charset=utf-8'
                            },
                            body: JSON.stringify({
                                student: this.studentContext,
                                settings: this.generationSettings,
                                prompt: this.promptBuilder
                            })
                        });
                        
                        if (!response.ok) {
                            throw new Error('ì½˜í…ì¸  ìƒì„± ìš”ì²­ ì‹¤íŒ¨');
                        }
                        
                        const result = await response.json();
                        this.generationResult.content = safeKoreanText(result.content);
                        this.generationResult.qualityScore = result.qualityScore || 0;
                        this.ui.activeTab = 'review';
                        
                    } catch (error) {
                        console.error('ì½˜í…ì¸  ìƒì„± ì˜¤ë¥˜:', error);
                        this.showError('ì½˜í…ì¸  ìƒì„± ì¤‘ ì˜¤ë¥˜ê°€ ë°œìƒí–ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.');
                    } finally {
                        this.generationResult.isGenerating = false;
                        this.generationResult.progress = 100;
                    }
                },
                
                // ì˜¤ë¥˜ í‘œì‹œ
                showError(message) {
                    this.generationResult.errors.push({
                        message: safeKoreanText(message),
                        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
                    });
                }
            }));
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>
```

```html
    <!-- Alpine.js ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸ -->
    <script>
        // UTF-8 ì•ˆì „ì„± í™•ë³´ í•¨ìˆ˜
        function validateUTF8Text(text) {
            try {
                const encoded = new TextEncoder().encode(text);
                const decoded = new TextDecoder('utf-8', { fatal: true }).decode(encoded);
                return decoded === text;
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('UTF-8 ì¸ì½”ë”© ì˜¤ë¥˜:', error);
                return false;
            }
        }

        // í•œê¸€ í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì•ˆì „ ì²˜ë¦¬
        function safeKoreanText(text) {
            return validateUTF8Text(text) ? text : text.replace(/[\u0000-\u001F\u007F-\u009F]/g, '');
        }

        // í’ˆì§ˆ ê´€ë¦¬ ìƒíƒœ ê´€ë¦¬
        document.addEventListener('alpine:init', () => {
            Alpine.data('qualityManagementData', () => ({
                ...qualityManagementData,
                
                // ìƒíƒœ í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ ë³€í™˜
                getStatusText(status) {
                    const statusMap = {
                        'pending': 'ê²€í†  ëŒ€ê¸°',
                        'in-review': 'ê²€í†  ì¤‘',
                        'approved': 'ìŠ¹ì¸ë¨',
                        'rejected': 'ë°˜ë ¤ë¨',
                        'revision-requested': 'ìˆ˜ì • ìš”ì²­'
                    };
                    return safeKoreanText(statusMap[status] || status);
                },
                
                // ë‚ ì§œ í¬ë§·íŒ…
                formatDate(dateString) {
                    return new Date(dateString).toLocaleDateString('ko-KR');
                },
                
                // ë¹ ë¥¸ ìŠ¹ì¸
                async quickApprove(item) {
                    try {
                        const response = await fetch(`/api/ai-tools/review/${item.id}/approve`, {
                            method: 'POST',
                            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json; charset=utf-8' }
                        });
                        if (response.ok) {
                            this.loadReviewQueue();
                        }
                    } catch (error) {
                        console.error('ìŠ¹ì¸ ì²˜ë¦¬ ì˜¤ë¥˜:', error);
                    }
                },
                
                // ë¹ ë¥¸ ë°˜ë ¤
                async quickReject(item) {
                    try {
                        const response = await fetch(`/api/ai-tools/review/${item.id}/reject`, {
                            method: 'POST',
                            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json; charset=utf-8' }
                        });
                        if (response.ok) {
                            this.loadReviewQueue();
                        }
                    } catch (error) {
                        console.error('ë°˜ë ¤ ì²˜ë¦¬ ì˜¤ë¥˜:', error);
                    }
                },
                
                // ê²€í†  ëŒ€ì—´ ë¡œë“œ
                async loadReviewQueue() {
                    try {
                        const response = await fetch('/api/ai-tools/review-queue', {
                            method: 'GET',
                            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json; charset=utf-8' }
                        });
                        const data = await response.json();
                        this.reviewQueue.items = data.items || [];
                        this.reviewQueue.totalCount = data.totalCount || 0;
                        this.reviewQueue.pendingCount = data.pendingCount || 0;
                    } catch (error) {
                        console.error('ê²€í†  ëŒ€ì—´ ë¡œë“œ ì˜¤ë¥˜:', error);
                    }
                }
            }));
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>
```

#### ì£¼ìš” íŠ¹ì§•

- **3ë‹¨ê³„ ê²€í†  ê³¼ì •**: ëŒ€ì—´ â†’ ì§€í‘œ â†’ ì„¤ì • ê´€ë¦¬
- **ë¹ ë¥¸ ì•¡ì…˜**: ìŠ¹ì¸/ë°˜ë ¤/ìˆ˜ì •ìš”ì²­ (48px ë²„íŠ¼)
- **ì ‘ê·¼ì„± ì¤€ìˆ˜**: ARIA ë ˆì´ë¸”, í‚¤ë³´ë“œ ë„¤ë¹„ê²Œì´ì…˜
- **UTF-8 ì•ˆì „ì„±**: í•œê¸€ í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì²˜ë¦¬ ì‹œ ì¸ì½”ë”© ê²€ì¦
- **HTMX í†µí•©**: ì‹¤ì‹œê°„ ë°ì´í„° ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸
- **Supabase Edge Functions**: ë°±ì—”ë“œ ê²€í†  ì²˜ë¦¬
- **Chart.js ì—°ë™**: í’ˆì§ˆ ì§€í‘œ ì‹œê°í™”

### 5.4 AI í•™ìŠµ ì§„ë‹¨ ë„êµ¬
**ê²½ë¡œ**: `/ai-tools/learning-diagnosis.html`
**íŒŒì¼**: `ai-tools/learning-diagnosis.html`

#### ì£¼ìš” ê¸°ëŠ¥
- í•™ìŠµ íŒ¨í„´ ë¶„ì„
- ê°•ì /ì•½ì  ì§„ë‹¨
- ë§ì¶¤í˜• ê°œì„  ì œì•ˆ
- í•™ìŠµ ê²½ë¡œ ìµœì í™”
- ì˜ˆì¸¡ ëª¨ë¸ë§

#### Alpine.js ë°ì´í„° êµ¬ì¡°
```javascript
// AI í•™ìŠµ ì§„ë‹¨ ìƒíƒœ ê´€ë¦¬
const learningDiagnosisData = {
  // í•™ìƒ ì„ íƒ ë° ê¸°ë³¸ ì •ë³´
  selectedStudent: null,
  studentInfo: {
    id: '',
    name: '',
    grade: '',
    disabilities: [],
    learningProfile: {}
  },
  
  // ì§„ë‹¨ ì„¤ì •
  diagnosisSettings: {
    analysisType: 'comprehensive', // comprehensive, focused, quick
    analysisPeriod: {
      startDate: '',
      endDate: '',
      preset: 'last-month' // last-week, last-month, last-semester
    },
    focusAreas: [], // academic, behavioral, social, motor
    includeComparisons: true
  },
  
  // ë°ì´í„° ì…ë ¥
  inputData: {
    assessmentData: { completed: false },
    behaviorObservations: { completed: false },
    learningLogs: { completed: false }
  },
  
  // ë¶„ì„ ê²°ê³¼
  analysisResults: {
    isAnalyzing: false,
    progress: 0,
    completed: false,
    strengthsWeaknesses: { strengths: [], weaknesses: [] },
    recommendations: { immediate: [], shortTerm: [], longTerm: [] }
  },
  
  // UI ìƒíƒœ
  ui: {
    currentStep: 1, // 1: setup, 2: data-input, 3: analysis, 4: results, 5: report
    showAdvanced: false,
    isGeneratingReport: false
  }
};
```

```html
    <!-- Alpine.js ìŠ¤í¬ë¦½íŠ¸ -->
    <script>
        // UTF-8 ì•ˆì „ì„± í™•ë³´
        function safeKoreanText(text) {
            return text.replace(/[\u0000-\u001F\u007F-\u009F]/g, '');
        }

        // í•™ìŠµ ì§„ë‹¨ ìƒíƒœ ê´€ë¦¬
        document.addEventListener('alpine:init', () => {
            Alpine.data('learningDiagnosisData', () => ({
                ...learningDiagnosisData,
                
                // AI ë¶„ì„ ì‹œì‘
                async startAnalysis() {
                    this.analysisResults.isAnalyzing = true;
                    this.analysisResults.progress = 0;
                    
                    try {
                        const response = await fetch('/api/ai-tools/analyze-learning', {
                            method: 'POST',
                            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json; charset=utf-8' },
                            body: JSON.stringify({
                                student: this.studentInfo,
                                settings: this.diagnosisSettings,
                                inputData: this.inputData
                            })
                        });
                        
                        const result = await response.json();
                        this.analysisResults.strengthsWeaknesses = result.strengthsWeaknesses;
                        this.analysisResults.recommendations = result.recommendations;
                        this.analysisResults.completed = true;
                        
                    } catch (error) {
                        console.error('ë¶„ì„ ì˜¤ë¥˜:', error);
                    } finally {
                        this.analysisResults.isAnalyzing = false;
                    }
                },
                
                // ë³´ê³ ì„œ ìƒì„±
                async generateReport() {
                    this.ui.isGeneratingReport = true;
                    
                    try {
                        const response = await fetch('/api/ai-tools/generate-report', {
                            method: 'POST',
                            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json; charset=utf-8' },
                            body: JSON.stringify({
                                analysisResults: this.analysisResults,
                                reportSettings: this.reportSettings
                            })
                        });
                        
                        const blob = await response.blob();
                        const url = window.URL.createObjectURL(blob);
                        const a = document.createElement('a');
                        a.href = url;
                        a.download = `í•™ìŠµì§„ë‹¨ë³´ê³ ì„œ_${this.studentInfo.name}.${this.reportSettings.format}`;
                        a.click();
                        
                    } catch (error) {
                        console.error('ë³´ê³ ì„œ ìƒì„± ì˜¤ë¥˜:', error);
                    } finally {
                        this.ui.isGeneratingReport = false;
                    }
                }
            }));
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>
```

#### ì£¼ìš” íŠ¹ì§•

- **ë‹¤ì–‘í•œ ë°ì´í„° ì†ŒìŠ¤**: í‰ê°€ ë°ì´í„°, í–‰ë™ ê´€ì°°, í•™ìŠµ ê¸°ë¡ í†µí•©
- **ì‹œê°ì  ë¶„ì„ ê²°ê³¼**: Chart.js ê¸°ë°˜ íŒ¨í„´ ë° ì˜ˆì¸¡ ì°¨íŠ¸
- **ë§ì¶¤í˜• ë³´ê³ ì„œ**: í…œí”Œë¦¿ ì„ íƒ, ì„¹ì…˜ ì»¤ìŠ¤í„°ë§ˆì´ì§•, ë‹¤ì–‘í•œ ì¶œë ¥ í˜•ì‹
- **ì‹¤ì‹œê°„ ì§„í–‰ìƒí™©**: ë¶„ì„ ì§„í–‰ë¥  ì‹¤ì‹œê°„ í‘œì‹œ
- **ì ‘ê·¼ì„± ì¤€ìˆ˜**: ARIA ë ˆì´ë¸”, ë‹¨ê³„ë³„ ë„¤ë¹„ê²Œì´ì…˜
- **UTF-8 ì•ˆì „ì„±**: í•œê¸€ í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì²˜ë¦¬ ì•ˆì „ì„± í™•ë³´
- **HTMX í†µí•©**: íŒŒì¼ ì—…ë¡œë“œ, ë°ì´í„° ë™ê¸°í™”
- **Supabase Edge Functions**: AI ë¶„ì„ ë° ë³´ê³ ì„œ ìƒì„± ë°±ì—”ë“œ

```javascript
<AIHistoryPage>
  <HistoryFilters>
    <DateRangeFilter />         // ë‚ ì§œ ë²”ìœ„
    <GenerationTypeFilter />    // ìƒì„± ìœ í˜•
    <UserFilter />              // ì‚¬ìš©ì í•„í„°
    <QualityFilter />           // í’ˆì§ˆ í•„í„°
  </HistoryFilters>
```

```html
<!-- Alpine.js ì»´í¬ë„ŒíŠ¸ ë¡œì§ -->
<script>
function footerComponent() {
  return {
    companyDescription: 'IEPONì€ ë°œë‹¬ì¥ì•  í•™ìƒì„ ìœ„í•œ ë§ì¶¤í˜• êµìœ¡ í”Œë«í¼ì…ë‹ˆë‹¤.',
    copyrightText: 'Â© 2024 IEPON. All rights reserved.',
    companyAddress: 'ì„œìš¸íŠ¹ë³„ì‹œ ê°•ë‚¨êµ¬ í…Œí—¤ë€ë¡œ 123, 456í˜¸',
    
    initFooter() {
      this.validateUTF8Content();
      this.setupAccessibilityFeatures();
    },
    
    getCurrentYear() {
      return `Â© ${new Date().getFullYear()} IEPON. All rights reserved.`;
    },
    
    validateUTF8Content() {
      const textElements = this.$el.querySelectorAll('[x-text]');
      textElements.forEach(element => {
        const text = element.textContent;
        if (text && !this.isValidUTF8(text)) {
          console.warn('UTF-8 ì¸ì½”ë”© ë¬¸ì œ:', text);
          element.textContent = 'í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ ë¡œë”© ì¤‘...';
        }
      });
    },
    
    isValidUTF8(text) {
      try {
        const encoded = new TextEncoder().encode(text);
        const decoded = new TextDecoder('utf-8', { fatal: true }).decode(encoded);
        return decoded === text;
      } catch (error) {
        return false;
      }
    },
    
    setupAccessibilityFeatures() {
      // í‚¤ë³´ë“œ ë„¤ë¹„ê²Œì´ì…˜ í–¥ìƒ
      const links = this.$el.querySelectorAll('a');
      links.forEach(link => {
        if (!link.getAttribute('aria-label')) {
          const text = link.textContent.trim();
          link.setAttribute('aria-label', `${text} í˜ì´ì§€ë¡œ ì´ë™`);
        }
      });
    }
  };
}
</script>
```

### 10.4 ëª¨ë‹¬ ë° ë‹¤ì´ì–¼ë¡œê·¸
**ê²½ë¡œ**: ì „ì—­ ì»´í¬ë„ŒíŠ¸
**íŒŒì¼**: `components/ui/modal.html`

#### ì£¼ìš” ê¸°ëŠ¥
- ë‹¤ì–‘í•œ í¬ê¸° ì˜µì…˜ (small, medium, large, fullscreen)
- ë¶€ë“œëŸ¬ìš´ ì—´ê¸°/ë‹«ê¸° ì• ë‹ˆë©”ì´ì…˜
- ë°°ê²½ í´ë¦­ìœ¼ë¡œ ë‹«ê¸°
- ESC í‚¤ë¡œ ë‹«ê¸° 
- í¬ì»¤ìŠ¤ íŠ¸ë˜í•‘ (ì ‘ê·¼ì„±)
- UTF-8 ì•ˆì „ í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ í‘œì‹œ
- WCAG 2.1 AA ì¤€ìˆ˜

#### HTML + Alpine.js êµ¬ì¡°
```html
<!-- ê¸°ë³¸ ëª¨ë‹¬ ì»´í¬ë„ŒíŠ¸ -->
<div class="modal-container" 
     x-data="modalComponent()" 
     x-show="isOpen" 
     x-cloak
     x-trap="isOpen"
     @keydown.escape="closeModal()"
     @click.self="closeModal()">
     
  <!-- ëª¨ë‹¬ ì˜¤ë²„ë ˆì´ -->
  <div class="modal-overlay" 
       x-show="isOpen"
       x-transition:enter="transition ease-out duration-300"
       x-transition:enter-start="opacity-0"
       x-transition:enter-end="opacity-100"
       x-transition:leave="transition ease-in duration-200"
       x-transition:leave-start="opacity-100"
       x-transition:leave-end="opacity-0">
    
    <!-- ëª¨ë‹¬ ì»¨í…Œì´ë„ˆ -->
    <div class="modal-content" 
         :class="`modal-${size}`"
         x-show="isOpen"
         x-transition:enter="transition ease-out duration-300 transform"
         x-transition:enter-start="opacity-0 translate-y-4 sm:translate-y-0 sm:scale-95"
         x-transition:enter-end="opacity-100 translate-y-0 sm:scale-100"
         x-transition:leave="transition ease-in duration-200 transform"
         x-transition:leave-start="opacity-100 translate-y-0 sm:scale-100"
         x-transition:leave-end="opacity-0 translate-y-4 sm:translate-y-0 sm:scale-95"
         role="dialog"
         :aria-labelledby="titleId"
         :aria-describedby="bodyId">
         
      <!-- ëª¨ë‹¬ í—¤ë” -->
      <div class="modal-header">
        <h2 :id="titleId" 
            class="modal-title" 
            x-text="title"></h2>
        <button type="button" 
                class="modal-close-button" 
                @click="closeModal()"
                aria-label="ëª¨ë‹¬ ë‹«ê¸°"
                style="min-height: 48px; min-width: 48px;">
          <svg class="close-icon" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" height="24">
            <path d="M19 6.41L17.59 5 12 10.59 6.41 5 5 6.41 10.59 12 5 17.59 6.41 19 12 13.41 17.59 19 19 17.59 13.41 12z"/>
          </svg>
        </button>
      </div>
      
      <!-- ëª¨ë‹¬ ë³¸ë¬¸ -->
      <div :id="bodyId" class="modal-body">
        <div class="modal-content-text" 
             x-html="content"
             x-init="validateContent()"></div>
      </div>
      
      <!-- ëª¨ë‹¬ í‘¸í„° (ì˜µì…˜) -->
      <div class="modal-footer" x-show="showFooter">
        <div class="modal-actions">
          <button type="button" 
                  class="modal-button cancel-button"
                  @click="onCancel()"
                  x-show="showCancel"
                  style="min-height: 48px; min-width: 120px;"
                  x-text="cancelText"></button>
          <button type="button" 
                  class="modal-button confirm-button"
                  @click="onConfirm()"
                  x-show="showConfirm"
                  style="min-height: 48px; min-width: 120px;"
                  x-text="confirmText"></button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

<!-- í™•ì¸ ëª¨ë‹¬ (ì‚­ì œ, ê²½ê³  ë“±) -->
<div class="confirmation-modal"
     x-data="confirmationModalComponent()" 
     x-show="isOpen" 
     x-cloak
     x-trap="isOpen"
     @keydown.escape="closeModal()">
     
  <div class="modal-overlay" @click.self="closeModal()">
    <div class="modal-content modal-small" role="alertdialog">
      
      <!-- ê²½ê³  ì•„ì´ì½˜ -->
      <div class="modal-icon warning-icon">
        <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="48" height="48" class="warning-svg">
          <path d="M1 21h22L12 2 1 21zm12-3h-2v-2h2v2zm0-4h-2v-4h2v4z" fill="#f56565"/>
        </svg>
      </div>
      
      <!-- í™•ì¸ ë©”ì‹œì§€ -->
      <div class="modal-body text-center">
        <h3 class="confirmation-title" x-text="title"></h3>
        <p class="confirmation-message" x-text="message"></p>
      </div>
      
      <!-- ì•¡ì…˜ ë²„íŠ¼ -->
      <div class="modal-footer">
        <div class="action-buttons">
          <button type="button" 
                  class="modal-button danger-button"
                  @click="onConfirm()"
                  style="min-height: 48px; min-width: 120px;"
                  x-text="confirmText"></button>
          <button type="button" 
                  class="modal-button cancel-button"

                  x-text="cancelText"></button>

<!-- í¼ ëª¨ë‹¬ -->
<div class="form-modal"
     x-data="formModalComponent()" 
     x-show="isOpen" 
     x-cloak
     x-trap="isOpen">
     
  <div class="modal-overlay">
    <div class="modal-content modal-large">
      
      <!-- í¼ ëª¨ë‹¬ í—¤ë” -->
      <div class="modal-header">
        <h2 class="modal-title" x-text="title"></h2>
        <button type="button" 
                class="modal-close-button" 
                @click="closeModal()"
                aria-label="ëª¨ë‹¬ ë‹«ê¸°"
                style="min-height: 48px; min-width: 48px;">
          <svg class="close-icon" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="24" height="24">
            <path d="M19 6.41L17.59 5 12 10.59 6.41 5 5 6.41 10.59 12 5 17.59 6.41 19 12 13.41 17.59 19 19 17.59 13.41 12z"/>
          </svg>
        </button>
      </div>
      
      <!-- í¼ ì½˜í…ì¸  -->
      <div class="modal-body">
        <form @submit.prevent="onSubmit()" x-ref="modalForm">
          <div class="form-fields" x-html="formFields"></div>
          <div class="form-validation" x-show="hasErrors">
            <ul class="error-list">
              <template x-for="error in errors" :key="error.field">
                <li class="error-item" x-text="error.message"></li>
              </template>
            </ul>
          </div>
        </form>
      </div>
      
      <!-- í¼ ì•¡ì…˜ -->
      <div class="modal-footer">
        <div class="modal-actions">
          <button type="button" 
                  class="modal-button cancel-button"
                  @click="closeModal()"
                  style="min-height: 48px; min-width: 120px;">ì·¨ì†Œ</button>
          <button type="submit" 
                  class="modal-button confirm-button"
                  @click="onSubmit()"
                  :disabled="isSubmitting"
                  style="min-height: 48px; min-width: 120px;">
            <span x-show="!isSubmitting" x-text="submitText"></span>
            <span x-show="isSubmitting">ì²˜ë¦¬ ì¤‘...</span>
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

<!-- ì •ë³´ ëª¨ë‹¬ -->
<div class="info-modal"
     x-data="infoModalComponent()" 
     x-show="isOpen" 
     x-cloak
     x-trap="isOpen">
     
  <div class="modal-overlay" @click.self="closeModal()">
    <div class="modal-content modal-medium">
      
      <!-- ì •ë³´ ì•„ì´ì½˜ -->
      <div class="modal-icon info-icon">
        <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="48" height="48" class="info-svg">
          <path d="M12,2A10,10 0 0,0 2,12A10,10 0 0,0 12,22A10,10 0 0,0 22,12A10,10 0 0,0 12,2M11,7H13V9H11V7M11,11H13V17H11V11Z" fill="#4299e1"/>
        </svg>
      </div>
      
      <!-- ì •ë³´ ì½˜í…ì¸  -->
      <div class="modal-body text-center">
        <h3 class="info-title" x-text="title"></h3>
        <div class="info-content" x-html="content"></div>
      </div>
      
      <!-- ë‹«ê¸° ë²„íŠ¼ -->
      <div class="modal-footer">
        <button type="button" 
                class="modal-button primary-button"
                @click="closeModal()"
                style="min-height: 48px; min-width: 120px;">í™•ì¸</button>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>

<!-- Alpine.js ëª¨ë‹¬ ì»´í¬ë„ŒíŠ¸ ë¡œì§ -->
<script>
function modalComponent() {
  return {
    isOpen: false,
    title: '',
    content: '',
    size: 'medium',
    showFooter: true,
    showCancel: true,
    showConfirm: true,
    cancelText: 'ì·¨ì†Œ',
    confirmText: 'í™•ì¸',
    titleId: 'modal-title-' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9),
    bodyId: 'modal-body-' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 9),
    
    openModal(config = {}) {
      Object.assign(this, config);
      this.isOpen = true;
      this.$nextTick(() => {
        this.focusFirstElement();
      });
    },
    
    closeModal() {
      this.isOpen = false;
      this.$dispatch('modal-closed');
    },
    
    onCancel() {
      this.closeModal();
      this.$dispatch('modal-cancelled');
    },
    
    onConfirm() {
      this.$dispatch('modal-confirmed');
      this.closeModal();
    },
    
    validateContent() {
      if (this.content && !this.isValidUTF8(this.content)) {
        console.warn('UTF-8 ì¸ì½”ë”© ë¬¸ì œ:', this.content);
        this.content = 'ì½˜í…ì¸  ë¡œë”© ì¤‘...';
      }
    },
    
    isValidUTF8(text) {
      try {
        const encoded = new TextEncoder().encode(text);
        const decoded = new TextDecoder('utf-8', { fatal: true }).decode(encoded);
        return decoded === text;
      } catch (error) {
        return false;
      }
    },
    
    focusFirstElement() {
      const firstFocusable = this.$el.querySelector('button, [href], input, select, textarea, [tabindex]:not([tabindex="-1"])');
      if (firstFocusable) {
        firstFocusable.focus();
      }
    }
  };
}

function confirmationModalComponent() {
  return {
    ...modalComponent(),
    title: 'í™•ì¸ í•„ìš”',
    message: 'ì´ ì‘ì—…ì„ ê³„ì†í•˜ì‹œê² ìŠµë‹ˆê¹Œ?',
    confirmText: 'í™•ì¸',
    cancelText: 'ì·¨ì†Œ'
  };
}

function formModalComponent() {
  return {
    ...modalComponent(),
    formFields: '',
    errors: [],
    hasErrors: false,
    isSubmitting: false,
    submitText: 'ì €ì¥',
    
    onSubmit() {
      this.isSubmitting = true;
      this.hasErrors = false;
      this.errors = [];
      
      // í¼ ìœ íš¨ì„± ê²€ì‚¬
      const form = this.$refs.modalForm;
      if (form && !form.checkValidity()) {
        this.isSubmitting = false;
        this.hasErrors = true;
        return;
      }
      
      this.$dispatch('modal-form-submit', {
        formData: new FormData(form)
      });
    }
  };
}

function infoModalComponent() {
  return {
    ...modalComponent(),
    showFooter: true,
    showCancel: false,
    showConfirm: false
  };
}
</script>
```

```html
<!-- Alpine.js í† ìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì»´í¬ë„ŒíŠ¸ ë¡œì§ -->
<script>
function toastContainer() {
  return {
    toasts: [],
    maxToasts: 5,
    defaultDuration: 5000, // 5ì´ˆ
    
    initToasts() {
      // ì „ì—­ ì´ë²¤íŠ¸ ë¦¬ìŠ¤ë„ˆ ë“±ë¡
      window.addEventListener('show-toast', (event) => {
        this.addToast(event.detail);
      });
    },
    
    addToast(config) {
      const toast = {
        id: Date.now() + Math.random(),
        type: config.type || 'info',
        title: config.title || '',
        message: config.message || '',
        actionText: config.actionText || null,
        duration: config.duration || this.defaultDuration,
        showProgress: config.showProgress !== false,
        visible: false,
        progress: 100
      };
      
      // UTF-8 ì•ˆì „ì„± ê²€ì‚¬
      if (!this.isValidUTF8(toast.message)) {
        toast.message = 'ë©”ì‹œì§€ ë¡œë”© ì˜¤ë¥˜';
        console.warn('UTF-8 ì¸ì½”ë”© ë¬¸ì œ:', config.message);
      }
      
      // ìµœëŒ€ ê°œìˆ˜ ì²´í¬
      if (this.toasts.length >= this.maxToasts) {
        this.removeToast(this.toasts[0].id);
      }
      
      this.toasts.push(toast);
      
      this.$nextTick(() => {
        toast.visible = true;
        this.startProgressTimer(toast);
      });
    },
    
    removeToast(id) {
      const index = this.toasts.findIndex(t => t.id === id);
      if (index !== -1) {
        this.toasts[index].visible = false;
        setTimeout(() => {
          this.toasts.splice(index, 1);
        }, 200); // ì• ë‹ˆë©”ì´ì…˜ ì™„ë£Œ ëŒ€ê¸°
      }
    },
    
    startProgressTimer(toast) {
      if (!toast.showProgress || toast.duration === 0) return;
      
      const interval = 100; // 0.1ì´ˆë§ˆë‹¤ ì—…ë°ì´íŠ¸
      const steps = toast.duration / interval;
      let currentStep = steps;
      
      const timer = setInterval(() => {
        currentStep--;
        toast.progress = (currentStep / steps) * 100;
        
        if (currentStep <= 0) {
          clearInterval(timer);
          this.removeToast(toast.id);
        }
      }, interval);
    },
    
    onToastAction(toast) {
      this.$dispatch('toast-action', {
        toastId: toast.id,
        actionType: toast.actionText
      });
      this.removeToast(toast.id);
    },
    
    isValidUTF8(text) {
      try {
        const encoded = new TextEncoder().encode(text);
        const decoded = new TextDecoder('utf-8', { fatal: true }).decode(encoded);
        return decoded === text;
      } catch (error) {
        return false;
      }
    }
  };
}

// ì „ì—­ í† ìŠ¤íŠ¸ í—¬í¼ í•¨ìˆ˜
window.showToast = function(config) {
  window.dispatchEvent(new CustomEvent('show-toast', {
    detail: config
  }));
};

// ì‚¬ìš© ì˜ˆì‹œ:
// showToast({ type: 'success', title: 'ì„±ê³µ', message: 'ì €ì¥ë˜ì—ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.' });
// showToast({ type: 'error', title: 'ì˜¤ë¥˜', message: 'ì‹œìŠ¤í…œ ì˜¤ë¥˜ê°€ ë°œìƒí–ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.' });
</script>
```

#### ì£¼ìš” ê¸°ëŠ¥
- ë‹¤ì–‘í•œ ë¡œë”© ì• ë‹ˆë©”ì´ì…˜ (ìŠ¤í”¼ë„ˆ, íìŠ¤, ë‡, íŒŒìš°ìŠ¤)
- ìŠ¤ì¼ˆë ˆí†¤ UI í‘œì‹œ (ì¹´ë“œ, ë¦¬ìŠ¤íŠ¸, í…Œì´ë¸”)
- í”„ë¡œê·¸ë ˆìŠ¤ ë°” í‘œì‹œ
- ì „ì²´ í™”ë©´ ë¡œë”© ì˜¤ë²„ë ˆì´
- ì¸ë¼ì¸ ë¡œë”© ìƒíƒœ
- UTF-8 ì•ˆì „ ë©”ì‹œì§€ í‘œì‹œ
- ì ‘ê·¼ì„± ì§€ì› (ARIA live regions)

#### HTML + Alpine.js êµ¬ì¡°

```html
<!-- ë¡œë”© ìŠ¤í”¼ë„ˆ -->
<div class="loading-spinner" 
     x-data="loadingSpinner()" 
     x-show="isLoading"
     x-cloak
     role="status"
     :aria-label="loadingMessage">
     
  <div class="spinner-container">
    <!-- íšŒì „ ìŠ¤í”¼ë„ˆ -->
    <div class="spinner-icon" 
         :class="spinnerType"
         aria-hidden="true">
      <div class="spinner-circle"></div>
      <div class="spinner-circle"></div>
      <div class="spinner-circle"></div>
    </div>
    
    <!-- ë¡œë”© ë©”ì‹œì§€ -->
    <p class="loading-text" 
       x-text="loadingMessage"
       x-show="showMessage"></p>
       
    <!-- ì§„í–‰ë¥  í‘œì‹œ (ì˜µì…˜) -->
    <div class="loading-progress" x-show="showProgress">
      <div class="progress-bar">
        <div class="progress-fill" 
             :style="`width: ${progress}%`"></div>
      </div>
      <span class="progress-text" x-text="`${Math.round(progress)}%`"></span>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

<!-- ìŠ¤ì¼ˆë ˆí†¤ ë¡œë” -->

  <div class="skeleton-table" x-show="type === 'table'">

          <div class="skeleton-cell animate-pulse"></div>
        </template>
      </div>
    </template>
  </div>
</div>

<!-- í”„ë¡œê·¸ë ˆìŠ¤ ë°” -->
<div class="progress-bar-container" 
     x-data="progressBar()" 
     x-show="isVisible"
     role="progressbar"
     :aria-valuenow="progress"
     :aria-valuemin="0"
     :aria-valuemax="100"
     :aria-label="progressLabel">
     
  <div class="progress-wrapper">

           :style="`width: ${progress}%; background-color: ${getProgressColor()}`"

<!-- ì „ì²´ í™”ë©´ ë¡œë”© -->

<!-- Alpine.js ë¡œë”© ì»´í¬ë„ŒíŠ¸ ë¡œì§ -->
<script>
function loadingSpinner() {
  return {
    isLoading: false,
    loadingMessage: 'ë¡œë”© ì¤‘...',
    spinnerType: 'default',
    showMessage: true,
    showProgress: false,
    progress: 0,
    
    startLoading(config = {}) {
      Object.assign(this, config);
      this.isLoading = true;
      
      // UTF-8 ì•ˆì „ì„± ê²€ì‚¬
      if (!this.isValidUTF8(this.loadingMessage)) {
        this.loadingMessage = 'ë¡œë”© ì¤‘...';
        console.warn('UTF-8 ì¸ì½”ë”© ë¬¸ì œ:', config.loadingMessage);
      }
    },
    
    stopLoading() {
      this.isLoading = false;
    },
    
    setProgress(value) {
      this.progress = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, value));
    },
    
    isValidUTF8(text) {
      try {
        const encoded = new TextEncoder().encode(text);
        const decoded = new TextDecoder('utf-8', { fatal: true }).decode(encoded);
        return decoded === text;
      } catch (error) {
        return false;
      }
    }
  };
}

function skeletonLoader() {
  return {
    isLoading: false,
    type: 'card', // 'card', 'list', 'table'
    itemCount: 3,
    columnCount: 4,
    rowCount: 5,
    
    startSkeleton(config = {}) {
      Object.assign(this, config);
      this.isLoading = true;
    },
    
    stopSkeleton() {
      this.isLoading = false;
    }
  };
}

function progressBar() {
  return {
    isVisible: false,
    progress: 0,
    progressLabel: 'ì§„í–‰ ìƒíƒœ',
    progressText: '',
    showLabel: true,
    progressClass: '',
    
    startProgress(config = {}) {
      Object.assign(this, config);
      this.isVisible = true;
    },
    
    updateProgress(value, text = '') {
      this.progress = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, value));
      this.progressText = text || `${Math.round(this.progress)}% ì™„ë£Œ`;
    },
    
    completeProgress() {
      this.progress = 100;
      this.progressText = 'ì™„ë£Œ';
      setTimeout(() => {
        this.isVisible = false;
      }, 1000);
    },
    
    getProgressColor() {
      if (this.progress < 30) return '#ef4444'; // ë¹¨ê°„ìƒ‰
      if (this.progress < 70) return '#f59e0b'; // ì£¼í™©ìƒ‰
      return '#10b981'; // ì´ˆë¡ìƒ‰
    }
  };
}

function fullscreenLoading() {
  return {
    isLoading: false,
    title: 'ì²˜ë¦¬ ì¤‘...',
    loadingMessage: 'ì”ì‹œë§Œ ê¸°ë‹¤ë ¤ ì£¼ì„¸ìš”.',
    showProgress: false,
    progress: 0,
    progressText: '',
    
    startFullscreenLoading(config = {}) {
      Object.assign(this, config);
      this.isLoading = true;
      document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
    },
    
    stopFullscreenLoading() {
      this.isLoading = false;
      document.body.style.overflow = '';
    }
  };
}
</script>
```

### 10.7 ì—ëŸ¬ ë°”ìš´ë”ë¦¬
**ê²½ë¡œ**: ì „ì—­ ì»´í¬ë„ŒíŠ¸
**íŒŒì¼**: `components/ui/error-boundary.html`

#### ì£¼ìš” ê¸°ëŠ¥
- ì „ì—­ JavaScript ì—ëŸ¬ ìºì¹˜
- ì‚¬ìš©ì ì¹œí™”ì  ì—ëŸ¬ í‘œì‹œ
- ì—ëŸ¬ ë¦¬í¬íŒ… ë° ë¡œê¹…
- í˜ì´ì§€ ìƒˆë¡œê³ ì¹¨ ê¸°ëŠ¥
- í´ë°± UI ì œê³µ
- UTF-8 ì•ˆì „ ì—ëŸ¬ ë©”ì‹œì§€
- ì ‘ê·¼ì„± ì§€ì›

#### HTML + Alpine.js êµ¬ì¡°
```html
<!-- ì—ëŸ¬ ë°”ìš´ë”ë¦¬ ì»´í¬ë„ŒíŠ¸ -->
<div class="error-boundary" 
     x-data="errorBoundary()" 
     x-show="hasError"
     x-cloak
     role="alert"
     aria-live="assertive">
     
  <div class="error-fallback">
    <!-- ì—ëŸ¬ ì•„ì´ì½˜ -->
    <div class="error-icon">
      <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="64" height="64" class="error-svg">
        <path d="M12 2C6.48 2 2 6.48 2 12s4.48 10 10 10 10-4.48 10-10S17.52 2 12 2zm-2 15l-5-5 1.41-1.41L10 14.17l7.59-7.59L19 8l-9 9z" fill="#ef4444"/>
      </svg>
    </div>
    
    <!-- ì—ëŸ¬ ì œëª© -->
    <h2 class="error-title">ë¬¸ì œê°€ ë°œìƒí–ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤</h2>
    
    <!-- ì—ëŸ¬ ë©”ì‹œì§€ -->
    <div class="error-message">
      <p class="error-description" x-text="errorMessage"></p>
      <details class="error-details" x-show="showDetails">
        <summary>ê¸°ìˆ ì  ì„¸ë¶€ì‚¬í•­</summary>
        <pre class="error-stack" x-text="errorStack"></pre>
      </details>
    </div>
    
    <!-- ì—ëŸ¬ ì•¡ì…˜ ë²„íŠ¼ -->
    <div class="error-actions">
      <button type="button" 
              class="error-button refresh-button"
              @click="refreshPage()"
              style="min-height: 48px; min-width: 120px;">ìƒˆë¡œê³ ì¹¨</button>
      <button type="button" 
              class="error-button report-button"
              @click="reportError()"
              style="min-height: 48px; min-width: 120px;">ì—ëŸ¬ ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸</button>
      <button type="button" 
              class="error-button home-button"
              @click="goHome()"
              style="min-height: 48px; min-width: 120px;">í™ˆìœ¼ë¡œ</button>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

<!-- Alpine.js ì—ëŸ¬ ë°”ìš´ë”ë¦¬ ë¡œì§ -->
<script>
function errorBoundary() {
  return {
    hasError: false,
    errorMessage: '',
    errorStack: '',
    showDetails: false,
    
    init() {
      this.setupErrorHandlers();
    },
    
    setupErrorHandlers() {
      // JavaScript ëŸ°íƒ€ì„ ì—ëŸ¬ ìºì¹˜
      window.addEventListener('error', (event) => {
        this.handleError(event.error, event.message);
      });
      
      // Promise ê±°ë¶€ ì—ëŸ¬ ìºì¹˜
      window.addEventListener('unhandledrejection', (event) => {
        this.handleError(event.reason, 'Unhandled Promise Rejection');
      });
      
      // Alpine.js ì—ëŸ¬ ìºì¹˜
      document.addEventListener('alpine:error', (event) => {
        this.handleError(event.detail.error, 'Alpine.js Error');
      });
    },
    
    handleError(error, message = '') {
      console.error('Error caught by boundary:', error);
      
      this.errorMessage = this.sanitizeErrorMessage(message || error.message || 'ì•Œ ìˆ˜ ì—†ëŠ” ì˜¤ë¥˜ê°€ ë°œìƒí–ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.');
      this.errorStack = error.stack || '';
      this.hasError = true;
      
      // ì—ëŸ¬ ë¡œê¹…
      this.logError(error, message);
    },
    
    sanitizeErrorMessage(message) {
      // UTF-8 ì•ˆì „ì„± ê²€ì‚¬
      if (!this.isValidUTF8(message)) {
        return 'ì—ëŸ¬ ë©”ì‹œì§€ ë¡œë”© ì¤‘...';
      }
      
      // ë¯¼ê°í•œ ì •ë³´ ì œê±°
      return message
        .replace(/\b[A-Za-z0-9._%+-]+@[A-Za-z0-9.-]+\.[A-Z|a-z]{2,}\b/g, '[ì´ë©”ì¼]')
        .replace(/\b\d{3}-\d{3,4}-\d{4}\b/g, '[ì „í™”ë²ˆí˜¸]');
    },
    
    refreshPage() {
      window.location.reload();
    },
    
    reportError() {
      // ì—ëŸ¬ ë¦¬í¬íŒ… API í˜¸ì¶œ
      const errorData = {
        message: this.errorMessage,
        stack: this.errorStack,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        url: window.location.href,
        userAgent: navigator.userAgent
      };
      
      fetch('/api/error-report', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify(errorData)
      }).then(() => {
        window.showToast({
          type: 'success',
          title: 'ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ ì „ì†¡',
          message: 'ì—ëŸ¬ ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ê°€ ì„±ê³µì ìœ¼ë¡œ ì „ì†¡ë˜ì—ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.'
        });
      }).catch(() => {
        window.showToast({
          type: 'error',
          title: 'ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ ì‹¤íŒ¨',
          message: 'ì—ëŸ¬ ë¦¬í¬íŠ¸ ì „ì†¡ì— ì‹¤íŒ¨í–ˆìŠµë‹ˆë‹¤.'
        });
      });
    },
    
    goHome() {
      window.location.href = '/';
    },
    
    logError(error, message) {
      const logData = {
        level: 'error',
        message: message,
        error: error.toString(),
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        url: window.location.href
      };
      
      console.error('ErrorBoundary:', logData);
    },
    
    isValidUTF8(text) {
      try {
        const encoded = new TextEncoder().encode(text);
        const decoded = new TextDecoder('utf-8', { fatal: true }).decode(encoded);
        return decoded === text;
      } catch (error) {
        return false;
      }
    }
  };
}
</script>
```

### 10.8 ë¸Œë ˆë“œí¬ëŸ¼ ë„¤ë¹„ê²Œì´ì…˜
**ê²½ë¡œ**: ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œ ë‚´ ëª¨ë“  í˜ì´ì§€
**íŒŒì¼**: `components/navigation/breadcrumb.html`

#### ì£¼ìš” ê¸°ëŠ¥
- í˜„ì¬ ìœ„ì¹˜ ê³„ì¸µ êµ¬ì¡° ì‹œê°í™”
- ìƒìœ„ ê²½ë¡œë¡œ ë¹ ë¥¸ ë„¤ë¹„ê²Œì´ì…˜
- ëª¨ë°”ì¼ì—ì„œ ì¶•ì•½ í‘œì‹œ
- êµ¬ì¡°í™”ëœ ë°ì´í„° ë§ˆí¬ì—… (JSON-LD)
- ì ‘ê·¼ì„± ë¼ë²¨ë§ ë° í‚¤ë³´ë“œ ë„¤ë¹„ê²Œì´ì…˜
- UTF-8 ì•ˆì „ ê²½ë¡œëª… í‘œì‹œ

#### HTML + Alpine.js êµ¬ì¡°
```html
<!-- ë¸Œë ˆë“œí¬ëŸ¼ ë„¤ë¹„ê²Œì´ì…˜ -->
<nav class="breadcrumb-navigation" 
     x-data="breadcrumbComponent()" 
     x-init="initBreadcrumb()"
     role="navigation"
     aria-label="í˜„ì¬ ìœ„ì¹˜ ë„¤ë¹„ê²Œì´ì…˜">
     
  <!-- ë¸Œë ˆë“œí¬ëŸ¼ ë¦¬ìŠ¤íŠ¸ -->
  <ol class="breadcrumb-list" 
      itemscope 
      itemtype="https://schema.org/BreadcrumbList">
      
    <!-- í™ˆ ë§í¬ -->
    <li class="breadcrumb-item" 
        itemprop="itemListElement" 
        itemscope 
        itemtype="https://schema.org/ListItem">
      <a href="/" 
         class="breadcrumb-link home-link"
         itemprop="item"
         style="min-height: 48px; display: inline-flex; align-items: center;"
         aria-label="í™ˆìœ¼ë¡œ ì´ë™">
        <svg class="home-icon" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true">
          <path d="M10 20v-6h4v6h5v-8h3L12 3 2 12h3v8z"/>
        </svg>
        <span itemprop="name">í™ˆ</span>
      </a>
      <meta itemprop="position" content="1">
      <span class="breadcrumb-separator" aria-hidden="true">/</span>
    </li>
    
    <!-- ë™ì  ë¸Œë ˆë“œí¬ëŸ¼ ì•„ì´í…œë“¤ -->
    <template x-for="(item, index) in breadcrumbItems" :key="item.id">
      <li class="breadcrumb-item" 
          itemprop="itemListElement" 
          itemscope 
          itemtype="https://schema.org/ListItem"
          :class="{ 'current': item.isCurrent }">
          
        <!-- ë§í¬ ê°€ëŠ¥í•œ ì•„ì´í…œ -->
        <template x-if="!item.isCurrent">
          <a :href="item.url" 
             class="breadcrumb-link"
             itemprop="item"
             style="min-height: 48px; display: inline-flex; align-items: center;"
             :aria-label="`${item.name} í˜ì´ì§€ë¡œ ì´ë™`">
            <span itemprop="name" x-text="item.name"></span>
          </a>
        </template>
        
        <!-- í˜„ì¬ í˜ì´ì§€ (ë§í¬ ì—†ìŒ) -->
        <template x-if="item.isCurrent">
          <span class="breadcrumb-current" 
                itemprop="item"
                aria-current="page">
            <span itemprop="name" x-text="item.name"></span>
          </span>
        </template>
        
        <meta itemprop="position" :content="index + 2">
        
        <!-- êµ¬ë¶„ì (ë§ˆì§€ë§‰ ì•„ì´í…œì´ ì•„ë‹ ê²½ìš°) -->
        <span x-show="!item.isCurrent" 
              class="breadcrumb-separator" 
              aria-hidden="true">/</span>
      </li>
    </template>
  </ol>
  
  <!-- ëª¨ë°”ì¼ ì¶•ì•½ ë²„íŠ¼ -->
  <button x-show="showMobileToggle" 
          @click="toggleMobileView()" 
          class="breadcrumb-mobile-toggle"
          type="button"
          style="min-height: 48px; min-width: 48px;"
          :aria-label="mobileExpanded ? 'ë¸Œë ˆë“œí¬ëŸ¼ ì ‘ê¸°' : 'ë¸Œë ˆë“œí¬ëŸ¼ í¼ì¹˜ê¸°'">
    <svg class="toggle-icon" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="16" height="16">
      <path :d="mobileExpanded ? 'M7 14l5-5 5 5z' : 'M7 10l5 5 5-5z'"/>
    </svg>
  </button>
</nav>

<!-- êµ¬ì¡°í™”ëœ ë°ì´í„° (JSON-LD) -->
<script type="application/ld+json" x-text="generateStructuredData()" x-show="false"></script>

<!-- Alpine.js ë¸Œë ˆë“œí¬ëŸ¼ ì»´í¬ë„ŒíŠ¸ ë¡œì§ -->
<script>
function breadcrumbComponent() {
  return {
    breadcrumbItems: [],
    showMobileToggle: false,
    mobileExpanded: false,
    
    initBreadcrumb() {
      this.generateBreadcrumbItems();
      this.checkMobileView();
      this.setupResizeListener();
    },
    
    generateBreadcrumbItems() {
      // í˜„ì¬ ê²½ë¡œë¥¼ ê¸°ë°˜ìœ¼ë¡œ ë¸Œë ˆë“œí¬ëŸ¼ ìƒì„±
      const path = window.location.pathname;
      const segments = path.split('/').filter(segment => segment);
      
      this.breadcrumbItems = segments.map((segment, index) => {
        const isLast = index === segments.length - 1;
        const url = '/' + segments.slice(0, index + 1).join('/');
        const name = this.formatSegmentName(segment);
        
        return {
          id: `breadcrumb-${index}`,
          name: name,
          url: url,
          isCurrent: isLast
        };
      });
      
      // UTF-8 ì•ˆì „ì„± ê²€ì‚¬
      this.breadcrumbItems.forEach(item => {
        if (!this.isValidUTF8(item.name)) {
          item.name = 'í˜ì´ì§€';
          console.warn('UTF-8 ì¸ì½”ë”© ë¬¸ì œ:', item.name);
        }
      });
    },
    
    formatSegmentName(segment) {
      // URL ì„¸ê·¸ë¨¼íŠ¸ë¥¼ ì‚¬ìš©ì ì¹œí™”ì  ì´ë¦„ìœ¼ë¡œ ë³€í™˜
      const nameMap = {
        'dashboard': 'ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œ',
        'students': 'í•™ìƒ ê´€ë¦¬',
        'curriculum': 'êµìœ¡ê³¼ì •',
        'plans': 'êµìœ¡ ê³„íš',
        'reports': 'ë³´ê³ ì„œ',
        'settings': 'ì„¤ì •',
        'profile': 'í”„ë¡œí•„',
        'admin': 'ê´€ë¦¬ì',
        'analytics': 'ë¶„ì„',
        'billing': 'ê²°ì œ ê´€ë¦¬'
      };
      
      return nameMap[segment] || this.capitalizeFirst(segment.replace(/-/g, ' '));
    },
    
    capitalizeFirst(str) {
      return str.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + str.slice(1);
    },
    
    checkMobileView() {
      this.showMobileToggle = window.innerWidth < 768 && this.breadcrumbItems.length > 2;
    },
    
    toggleMobileView() {
      this.mobileExpanded = !this.mobileExpanded;
      
      // ëª¨ë°”ì¼ì—ì„œ í¼ì¹˜ê¸°/ì ‘ê¸° ì²˜ë¦¬
      const breadcrumbList = this.$el.querySelector('.breadcrumb-list');
      if (this.mobileExpanded) {
        breadcrumbList.classList.add('expanded');
      } else {
        breadcrumbList.classList.remove('expanded');
      }
    },
    
    setupResizeListener() {
      window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
        this.checkMobileView();
      });
    },
    
    generateStructuredData() {
      // JSON-LD êµ¬ì¡°í™”ëœ ë°ì´í„° ìƒì„±
      const itemListElement = [
        {
          '@type': 'ListItem',
          position: 1,
          name: 'í™ˆ',
          item: window.location.origin + '/'
        },
        ...this.breadcrumbItems.map((item, index) => ({
          '@type': 'ListItem',
          position: index + 2,
          name: item.name,
          item: window.location.origin + item.url
        }))
      ];
      
      return JSON.stringify({
        '@context': 'https://schema.org',
        '@type': 'BreadcrumbList',
        itemListElement: itemListElement
      });
    },
    
    isValidUTF8(text) {
      try {
        const encoded = new TextEncoder().encode(text);
        const decoded = new TextDecoder('utf-8', { fatal: true }).decode(encoded);
        return decoded === text;
      } catch (error) {
        return false;
      }
    }
  };
}
</script>
```

### 10.9 í˜ì´ì§€ ë ˆì´ì•„ì›ƒ
**ê²½ë¡œ**: ì „ì—­ ë ˆì´ì•„ì›ƒ
**íŒŒì¼**: `components/layout/page-layout.html`

#### ì£¼ìš” ê¸°ëŠ¥
- ì‹œë§¨í‹±í•œ HTML5 í˜ì´ì§€ êµ¬ì¡°
- ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œ/ì¼ë°˜ í˜ì´ì§€ ë ˆì´ì•„ì›ƒ ë³€í™˜
- ëª¨ë°”ì¼ ë°˜ì‘í˜• ë ˆì´ì•„ì›ƒ
- í—¤ë”/ì‚¬ì´ë“œë°”/ë©”ì¸ì½˜í…ì¸ /í‘¸í„° ì˜ì—­ ê´€ë¦¬
- WCAG 2.1 AA ì ‘ê·¼ì„± ëœë“œë§ˆí¬
- ì‚¬ì´ë“œë°” í† ê¸€ ë° ì˜¤í”„ìº”ë²„ìŠ¤ ë©”ë‰´
- UTF-8 ì•ˆì „ ì½˜í…ì¸  ë Œë”ë§

#### HTML + Alpine.js êµ¬ì¡°
```html
<!-- ì „ì²´ í˜ì´ì§€ ë ˆì´ì•„ì›ƒ -->
<div class="page-layout" 
     x-data="pageLayoutComponent()" 
     x-init="initPageLayout()"
     :class="layoutClass">
     
  <!-- ìŠ¤í‚µ ë„¤ë¹„ê²Œì´ì…˜ (ì ‘ê·¼ì„±) -->
  <a href="#main-content" 
     class="skip-to-content"
     @focus="skipLinkVisible = true"
     @blur="skipLinkVisible = false"
     :class="{ 'visible': skipLinkVisible }">ë©”ì¸ ì½˜í…ì¸ ë¡œ ë°”ë¡œê°€ê¸°</a>
  
  <!-- í—¤ë” ì˜ì—­ -->
  <header class="page-header" 
          role="banner"
          x-data="headerComponent()">
          
    <!-- ë©”ì¸ ë„¤ë¹„ê²Œì´ì…˜ -->
    <nav class="main-navigation" 
         role="navigation" 
         aria-label="ë©”ì¸ ë„¤ë¹„ê²Œì´ì…˜">
         
      <!-- ë¡œê³  ë° ë¸Œëœë“œ -->
      <div class="brand-section">
        <a href="/" 
           class="brand-link"
           style="min-height: 48px; display: inline-flex; align-items: center;"
           aria-label="IEPON í™ˆìœ¼ë¡œ ì´ë™">
          <img src="/images/logo.png" 
               alt="IEPON ë¡œê³ " 
               class="brand-logo" 
               width="120" 
               height="40">
          <span class="brand-name">IEPON</span>
        </a>
      </div>
      
      <!-- ëª¨ë°”ì¼ ë©”ë‰´ í† ê¸€ ë²„íŠ¼ -->
      <button @click="toggleMobileMenu()" 
              class="mobile-menu-toggle"
              type="button"
              style="min-height: 48px; min-width: 48px;"
              :aria-label="mobileMenuOpen ? 'ë©”ë‰´ ë‹«ê¸°' : 'ë©”ë‰´ ì—´ê¸°'"
              :aria-expanded="mobileMenuOpen">
        <span class="hamburger-icon" :class="{ 'active': mobileMenuOpen }"></span>
      </button>
      
      <!-- ë„¤ë¹„ê²Œì´ì…˜ ë©”ë‰´ -->
      <ul class="nav-menu" 
          :class="{ 'mobile-open': mobileMenuOpen }"
          role="menubar">
        <template x-for="menuItem in navigationItems" :key="menuItem.id">
          <li class="nav-item" role="none">
            <a :href="menuItem.url" 
               class="nav-link"
               style="min-height: 48px; display: inline-flex; align-items: center;"
               :class="{ 'active': isCurrentPage(menuItem.url) }"
               :aria-label="`${menuItem.name} í˜ì´ì§€ë¡œ ì´ë™`"
               role="menuitem">
              <span class="nav-icon" x-html="menuItem.icon" aria-hidden="true"></span>
              <span class="nav-text" x-text="menuItem.name"></span>
            </a>
          </li>
        </template>
      </ul>
      
      <!-- ì‚¬ìš©ì ë©”ë‰´ -->
      <div class="user-menu" 
           x-data="{ userMenuOpen: false }"
           @click.away="userMenuOpen = false">
        <button @click="userMenuOpen = !userMenuOpen"
                class="user-menu-trigger"
                type="button"
                style="min-height: 48px;"
                :aria-label="userMenuOpen ? 'ì‚¬ìš©ì ë©”ë‰´ ë‹«ê¸°' : 'ì‚¬ìš©ì ë©”ë‰´ ì—´ê¸°'"
                :aria-expanded="userMenuOpen">
          <img :src="userProfile.avatar" 
               :alt="`${userProfile.name} í”„ë¡œí•„ ì‚¬ì§„`"
               class="user-avatar"
               width="32" 
               height="32">
          <span class="user-name" x-text="userProfile.name"></span>
        </button>
        
        <ul x-show="userMenuOpen" 
            x-transition:enter="transition ease-out duration-100"
            x-transition:enter-start="transform opacity-0 scale-95"
            x-transition:enter-end="transform opacity-100 scale-100"
            x-transition:leave="transition ease-in duration-75"
            x-transition:leave-start="transform opacity-100 scale-100"
            x-transition:leave-end="transform opacity-0 scale-95"
            class="user-dropdown"
            role="menu">
          <template x-for="userMenuItem in userMenuItems" :key="userMenuItem.id">
            <li role="none">
              <a :href="userMenuItem.url" 
                 class="user-menu-link"
                 style="min-height: 48px; display: flex; align-items: center;"
                 role="menuitem">
                <span class="menu-icon" x-html="userMenuItem.icon" aria-hidden="true"></span>
                <span x-text="userMenuItem.name"></span>
              </a>
            </li>
          </template>
        </ul>
      </div>
    </nav>
  </header>
  
  <!-- ë©”ì¸ ì½˜í…ì¸  ì˜ì—­ -->
  <main class="page-main" 
        role="main" 
        id="main-content"
        :class="{ 'with-sidebar': showSidebar }">
        
    <!-- ì‚¬ì´ë“œë°” (ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œ í˜ì´ì§€ë§Œ) -->
    <aside x-show="showSidebar" 
           x-transition:enter="transition ease-out duration-200"
           x-transition:enter-start="transform -translate-x-full"
           x-transition:enter-end="transform translate-x-0"
           x-transition:leave="transition ease-in duration-200"
           x-transition:leave-start="transform translate-x-0"
           x-transition:leave-end="transform -translate-x-full"
           class="page-sidebar" 
           role="complementary"
           aria-label="ë³´ì¡° ë„¤ë¹„ê²Œì´ì…˜">
           
      <!-- ì‚¬ì´ë“œë°” ì½˜í…ì¸ ëŠ” ê° í˜ì´ì§€ë³„ë¡œ ë™ì ìœ¼ë¡œ ë¡œë“œ -->
      <div x-html="sidebarContent"></div>
    </aside>
    
    <!-- ì½˜í…ì¸  ì˜ì—­ -->
    <div class="content-area">
      <!-- ë¸Œë ˆë“œí¬ëŸ¼ ë„¤ë¹„ê²Œì´ì…˜ -->
      <div x-show="showBreadcrumb" class="breadcrumb-wrapper">
        <!-- ë¸Œë ˆë“œí¬ëŸ¼ ì»´í¬ë„ŒíŠ¸ê°€ ì—¬ê¸°ì— ì‚½ì… -->
        <div x-html="breadcrumbContent"></div>
      </div>
      
      <!-- í˜ì´ì§€ íƒ€ì´í‹€ -->
      <div x-show="pageTitle" class="page-title-section">
        <h1 class="page-title" x-text="pageTitle"></h1>
        <p x-show="pageDescription" 
           class="page-description" 
           x-text="pageDescription"></p>
      </div>
      
      <!-- í˜ì´ì§€ ì½˜í…ì¸  -->
      <div class="page-content">
        <!-- ê° í˜ì´ì§€ì˜ ì‹¤ì œ ì½˜í…ì¸ ê°€ ì—¬ê¸°ì— ë Œë”ë§ -->
        <div x-html="pageContent"></div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </main>
  
  <!-- í‘¸í„° ì˜ì—­ -->
  <footer class="page-footer" 
          role="contentinfo" 
          x-show="showFooter">
    <!-- í‘¸í„° ì»´í¬ë„ŒíŠ¸ê°€ ì—¬ê¸°ì— ì‚½ì… -->
    <div x-html="footerContent"></div>
  </footer>
  
  <!-- ëª¨ë°”ì¼ ì˜¤ë²„ë ˆì´ -->
  <div x-show="mobileMenuOpen" 
       @click="closeMobileMenu()"
       x-transition:enter="transition ease-out duration-200"
       x-transition:enter-start="opacity-0"
       x-transition:enter-end="opacity-100"
       x-transition:leave="transition ease-in duration-150"
       x-transition:leave-start="opacity-100"
       x-transition:leave-end="opacity-0"
       class="mobile-overlay" 
       aria-hidden="true"></div>
</div>

<!-- Alpine.js í˜ì´ì§€ ë ˆì´ì•„ì›ƒ ì»´í¬ë„ŒíŠ¸ ë¡œì§ -->
<script>
function pageLayoutComponent() {
  return {
    // ë ˆì´ì•„ì›ƒ ìƒíƒœ
    layoutType: 'default', // 'default', 'dashboard', 'full-width'
    skipLinkVisible: false,
    mobileMenuOpen: false,
    showSidebar: false,
    showBreadcrumb: true,
    showFooter: true,
    
    // í˜ì´ì§€ ì •ë³´
    pageTitle: '',
    pageDescription: '',
    
    // ì½˜í…ì¸ 
    pageContent: '',
    sidebarContent: '',
    breadcrumbContent: '',
    footerContent: '',
    
    // ë„¤ë¹„ê²Œì´ì…˜ ì•„ì´í…œ
    navigationItems: [

      },
      {
        id: 'students',
        name: 'í•™ìƒ ê´€ë¦¬',

      },
      {
        id: 'curriculum',
        name: 'êµìœ¡ê³¼ì •',
        url: '/curriculum',
        icon: '<svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="20" height="20"><path d="M19 3H5c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h14c1.1 0 2-.9 2-2V5c0-1.1-.9-2-2-2zm-5 14H7v-2h7v2zm3-4H7v-2h10v2zm0-4H7V7h10v2z"/></svg>'
      }
    ],
    
    // ì‚¬ìš©ì ë©”ë‰´ ì•„ì´í…œ
    userMenuItems: [
      { id: 'profile', name: 'í”„ë¡œí•„', url: '/profile', icon: '<svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="16" height="16"><path d="M12 12c2.21 0 4-1.79 4-4s-1.79-4-4-4-4 1.79-4 4 1.79 4 4 4zm0 2c-2.67 0-8 1.34-8 4v2h16v-2c0-2.66-5.33-4-8-4z"/></svg>' },
      { id: 'settings', name: 'ì„¤ì •', url: '/settings', icon: '<svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="16" height="16"><path d="M19.14,12.94c0.04-0.3,0.06-0.61,0.06-0.94c0-0.32-0.02-0.64-0.07-0.94l2.03-1.58c0.18-0.14,0.23-0.41,0.12-0.61 l-1.92-3.32c-0.12-0.22-0.37-0.29-0.59-0.22l-2.39,0.96c-0.5-0.38-1.03-0.7-1.62-0.94L14.4,2.81c-0.04-0.24-0.24-0.41-0.48-0.41 h-3.84c-0.24,0-0.43,0.17-0.47,0.41L9.25,5.35C8.66,5.59,8.12,5.92,7.63,6.29L5.24,5.33c-0.22-0.08-0.47,0-0.59,0.22L2.74,8.87 C2.62,9.08,2.66,9.34,2.86,9.48l2.03,1.58C4.84,11.36,4.82,11.69,4.82,12s0.02,0.64,0.07,0.94l-2.03,1.58 c-0.18,0.14-0.23,0.41-0.12,0.61l1.92,3.32c0.12,0.22,0.37,0.29,0.59,0.22l2.39-0.96c0.5,0.38,1.03,0.7,1.62,0.94l0.36,2.54 c0.05,0.24,0.24,0.41,0.48,0.41h3.84c0.24,0,0.44-0.17,0.47-0.41l0.36-2.54c0.59-0.24,1.13-0.56,1.62-0.94l2.39,0.96 c0.22,0.08,0.47,0,0.59-0.22l1.92-3.32c0.12-0.22,0.07-0.47-0.12-0.61L19.14,12.94z M12,15.6c-1.98,0-3.6-1.62-3.6-3.6 s1.62-3.6,3.6-3.6s3.6,1.62,3.6,3.6S13.98,15.6,12,15.6z"/></svg>' },
      { id: 'logout', name: 'ë¡œê·¸ì•„ì›ƒ', url: '/logout', icon: '<svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="16" height="16"><path d="M17 7l-1.41 1.41L18.17 11H8v2h10.17l-2.58 2.58L17 17l5-5zM4 5h8V3H4c-1.1 0-2 .9-2 2v14c0 1.1.9 2 2 2h8v-2H4V5z"/></svg>' }
    ],
    
    // ì‚¬ìš©ì í”„ë¡œí•„
    userProfile: {
      name: 'ì‚¬ìš©ì',
      avatar: '/images/default-avatar.png'
    },
    
    get layoutClass() {
      return {
        'layout-default': this.layoutType === 'default',
        'layout-dashboard': this.layoutType === 'dashboard',
        'layout-full-width': this.layoutType === 'full-width',
        'mobile-menu-open': this.mobileMenuOpen
      };
    },
    
    initPageLayout() {
      this.detectLayoutType();
      this.loadUserProfile();
      this.loadPageContent();
      this.setupEventListeners();
    },
    
    detectLayoutType() {
      const path = window.location.pathname;
      if (path.startsWith('/dashboard')) {
        this.layoutType = 'dashboard';
        this.showSidebar = true;
      } else if (path.includes('/full-width')) {
        this.layoutType = 'full-width';
        this.showFooter = false;
      } else {
        this.layoutType = 'default';
      }
    },
    
    toggleMobileMenu() {
      this.mobileMenuOpen = !this.mobileMenuOpen;
      
      // ìŠ¤í¬ë¡¤ ë°©ì§€/í—ˆìš©
      if (this.mobileMenuOpen) {
        document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
      } else {
        document.body.style.overflow = '';
      }
    },
    
    closeMobileMenu() {
      this.mobileMenuOpen = false;
      document.body.style.overflow = '';
    },
    
    isCurrentPage(url) {
      return window.location.pathname === url || 
             window.location.pathname.startsWith(url + '/');
    },
    
    loadUserProfile() {
      // ì‚¬ìš©ì í”„ë¡œí•„ ì •ë³´ ë¡œë“œ (HTMX ë˜ëŠ” Alpine.storeì—ì„œ)
      const userStore = Alpine.store('auth');
      if (userStore && userStore.user) {
        this.userProfile = {
          name: userStore.user.name || 'ì‚¬ìš©ì',
          avatar: userStore.user.avatar || '/images/default-avatar.png'
        };
        
        // UTF-8 ì•ˆì „ì„± ê²€ì‚¬
        if (!this.isValidUTF8(this.userProfile.name)) {
          this.userProfile.name = 'ì‚¬ìš©ì';
          console.warn('ì‚¬ìš©ìëª… UTF-8 ì¸ì½”ë”© ë¬¸ì œ');
        }
      }
    },
    
    loadPageContent() {
      // ê° í˜ì´ì§€ë³„ ì½˜í…ì¸  ë¡œë“œ
      const path = window.location.pathname;
      
      // í˜ì´ì§€ë³„ íƒ€ì´í‹€ ì„¤ì •
      const pageTitles = {
        '/dashboard': 'ëŒ€ì‹œë³´ë“œ',
        '/students': 'í•™ìƒ ê´€ë¦¬',
        '/curriculum': 'êµìœ¡ê³¼ì •',
        '/plans': 'êµìœ¡ ê³„íš',
        '/reports': 'ë³´ê³ ì„œ',
        '/settings': 'ì„¤ì •'
      };
      
      this.pageTitle = pageTitles[path] || 'í˜ì´ì§€';
      
      // UTF-8 ì•ˆì „ì„± ê²€ì‚¬
      if (!this.isValidUTF8(this.pageTitle)) {
        this.pageTitle = 'í˜ì´ì§€';
      }
    },
    
    setupEventListeners() {
      // ë¦¬ì‚¬ì´ì¦ˆ ì´ë²¤íŠ¸
      window.addEventListener('resize', () => {
        if (window.innerWidth > 768) {
          this.closeMobileMenu();
        }
      });
      
      // ESC í‚¤ë¡œ ëª¨ë°”ì¼ ë©”ë‰´ ë‹«ê¸°
      window.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
        if (e.key === 'Escape' && this.mobileMenuOpen) {
          this.closeMobileMenu();
        }
      });
    },
    
    isValidUTF8(text) {
      try {
        const encoded = new TextEncoder().encode(text);
        const decoded = new TextDecoder('utf-8', { fatal: true }).decode(encoded);
        return decoded === text;
      } catch (error) {
        return false;
      }
    }
  };
}
</script>
```

### 10.10 ê³µí†µ í¼ ì»´í¬ë„ŒíŠ¸

#### ì£¼ìš” ê¸°ëŠ¥
- ì ‘ê·¼ì„± ê¸°ì¤€ ì…ë ¥ í•„ë“œ ì»´í¬ë„ŒíŠ¸
- ì‹¤ì‹œê°„ ìœ íš¨ì„± ê²€ì‚¬ ë° ë©”ì‹œì§€ í‘œì‹œ
- ì—ëŸ¬ ìƒíƒœ ì‹œê°í™” ë° ì•ˆë‚´

#### HTML + Alpine.js êµ¬ì¡°

##### 1. ê¸°ë³¸ í…ìŠ¤íŠ¸ ì…ë ¥ í•„ë“œ
```html
<div class="form-field" x-data="formFieldComponent()" x-init="initField()">
  <label class="field-label" :for="fieldId" :class="{ 'required': isRequired }">
    <span class="label-text" x-text="label"></span>
    <span x-show="isRequired" class="required-indicator">*</span>
  </label>
  
  <div class="input-container" :class="{ 'error': hasError }">
    <input :id="fieldId" :name="fieldName" :type="inputType" class="form-input" 
           style="min-height: 48px;" :value="fieldValue" @input="handleInput($event)" 
           @blur="validateField()" :placeholder="placeholder" :required="isRequired" 
           :aria-invalid="hasError" :aria-describedby="getAriaDescribedBy()">
  </div>
  
  <div class="field-help">
    <p x-show="helpText && !hasError" class="help-text" x-text="helpText"></p>
    <div x-show="hasError" class="error-message" role="alert">
      <span x-text="errorMessage"></span>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>
```

##### 2. ì…€ë ‰íŠ¸ ë“œë¡­ë‹¤ìš´
```html
<div class="select-field" x-data="selectComponent()" @click.away="closeDropdown()">
  <label class="field-label" :for="selectId">
    <span class="label-text" x-text="label"></span>
    <span x-show="isRequired" class="required-indicator">*</span>
  </label>
  
  <div class="select-container">
    <button type="button" :id="selectId" class="select-trigger" 
            style="min-height: 48px;" @click="toggleDropdown()" 
            :aria-expanded="isOpen">
      <span x-text="selectedOption ? selectedOption.label : placeholder"></span>
      <svg class="select-icon" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="20" height="20">
        <path d="M7 10l5 5 5-5z"/>
      </svg>
    </button>
    
    <ul x-show="isOpen" x-transition class="select-dropdown" role="listbox">
      <template x-for="option in options" :key="option.value">
        <li class="select-option" @click="selectOption(option)" 
            :class="{ 'selected': option.value === selectedValue }">
          <span x-text="option.label"></span>
        </li>
      </template>
    </ul>
  </div>
  
  <div x-show="hasError" class="error-message" role="alert">
    <span x-text="errorMessage"></span>
  </div>
</div>
```
